ANTC03H3 (20255) — Directed Reading in Anthropology
Enrollment
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been
granted. Check your status through ACORN to see whether you have been approved. (APP =
approval; REF = refused; INT = no decision yet)
Notes
SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled
until you complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'.

Ensure the course code, supervisor's name and title of the project is clearly printed on the form
as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Your Department listed below
may require additional paperwork. Students should contact the office listed for more
information.
Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form and additional paperwork by email to the
Program Advisor anthropologyadvisor.utsc@utoronto.ca
Program Advisor will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved
(APP).

CITC54H3 (F) — City Studies Field Trip Course
Enrollment
Enrolment Indicator: E
Enrolment via ACORN is not available. Students must request permission to enrol in this course
by contacting the sponsoring department.
Notes
CITC54H3 is a Field course. Interested students must contact the department for enrolment
into the course at cit-advisor@utsc.utoronto.ca.
The 2-week global studio “Planning the Inclusive City: Bogotá in Comparative Perspective” in
Bogotá will provide students with a hands-on learning experience about inclusive urban
planning in Colombia's capital. The studio will be hosted by the University of the Andes in
Bogotá, Colombia's top university, in collaboration with the University of Amsterdam
(Netherlands) and the University of Toronto, Scarborough (Canada) during June 9-20, 2025.
This summer course will provide students with an interdisciplinary and experiential perspective
on how to plan inclusive cities. With Bogotá as our classroom, participants will engage with
real-world problems by studying the controversial implementation of inclusive planning
initiatives regarding care infrastructure, accessibility and sustainable mobility, local economic
development, and urban governance.
Component Section Day Time Delivery Instructor
LEC 1 TH 11:00-13:00 INPER Montero Munoz, S.

given preference for further enrollment over non-CSC program students.

lecture will be accommodated in a tutorial. When the term starts, if necessary, additional

HLTD01H3 (20255) — Directed Readings in Health and Society
Enrollment
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been
granted. Check your status through ACORN to see whether you have been approved. (APP =
approval; REF = refused; INT = no decision yet)
Notes
SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled
until you complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Secure a faculty member as a supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised
Study form'. Ensure the course code, supervisor's name and title of the project is clearly
printed on the form as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study
form is available at: https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form.
Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form by email to Sean Ramrattan
sean.ramrattan@utoronto.ca one week prior to the last day to add courses for the session.
Staff will ensure your course status on ACORN will be updated from interim (INT) to approved
(APP).

enough to remain, the instructor will request that your status will be changed from INT to APP
through the departmental office.

course is processed. If a question is not applicable, indicate NA. If you encounter technical
difficulties at this step, click the hyperlinked 'Technical Support' at the bottom right of the
webpage or contact intranet@utsc.utoronto.ca
If you enroll or are admitted from the wait list after the deadline, you must fill out the
questionnaire and submit it to the course instructor.

interim (INT) to approved (APP).

MATD92H3 (20255) — Mathematics Project
Enrollment
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been
granted. Check your status through ACORN to see whether you have been approved. (APP =
approval; REF = refused; INT = no decision yet)
Notes
SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled
until you complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Email the CMS faculty member and obtain their approval, make sure the course code,
supervisor name, and title of the project is input on the form as this information will appear on
your transcript.
Step 3: Submit the approval email from the faculty member and the completed Supervised
Study form by email to Kelly Squier kelly.squier@utoronto.ca
The department will arrange to have your course status on ACORN changed from interim (INT)
to approved (APP).
The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Your Department may require
additional paperwork.

management courses during Summer 2025 may enroll in courses the usual way, but are
cautioned that they may be withdrawn from courses if there are continuing undergraduate
students on waitlists. Priority will be given to continuing undergraduate students who are
pursuing degree or program requirements. Please see Calendar for overall course load limit for
BBA students.

Notes

Priority is necessary, as co-op students must take specific Management courses in the Summer
in order to participate in the Fall/Winter work terms.
Students not in the program, including Minors in Economics, ARE REQUIRED to have a CGPA of
2.0 or better if they want to enroll in in MGEB02H3, MGEB06H3, MGEB11H3, MGEB12H3,
MGEC02H3, MGEC06H3, and MGEC11H3. At this time, all students (BBA, Major program and
non-program) will have equal access to the courses, or the opportunity to waitlist.
BBA students are no longer allowed to use STAB22H3 or STAB23H3 to fulfill program
requirements and they will be restricted from taking STAB22H3 and STAB23H3. BBA students
who have completed STAB22H3 after August 2012 or STAB23H3 ARE REQUIRED to take
MGEB11H3 as EXTRA before enrolling themselves into MGEB12H3
Which course will be open to Non-Program Students and When
Non-Program students (including Economics Minor students) may enroll in MGEA02H3,
MGEA06H3 and MGEC93H3 from the start of course enrolment.

SCSPE01332 - Specialist (Co-operative) Program in Economics for Management Studies
At 3:00pm on March 25, 2025, enrollment will open to students in the following groups:
MGT - All Management Students
Enrolment will open to all UTSC students on 6:00am on April 1, 2025. Enrolment will open to
UTSG and UTM students on 6:00am on April 8, 2025.
Notes

Management & Economics Co-op students have priority until 3pm on the first day of enrolment.
Priority is necessary, as co-op students must take specific Management courses in the Summer
in order to participate in the Fall/Winter work terms.
Students not in the program, including Minors in Economics, ARE REQUIRED to have a CGPA of
2.0 or better if they want to enroll in in MGEB02H3, MGEB06H3, MGEB11H3, MGEB12H3,
MGEC02H3, MGEC06H3, and MGEC11H3. At this time, all students (BBA, Major program and
non-program) will have equal access to the courses, or the opportunity to waitlist.
BBA students are no longer allowed to use STAB22H3 or STAB23H3 to fulfill program
requirements and they will be restricted from taking STAB22H3 and STAB23H3. BBA students
who have completed STAB22H3 after August 2012 or STAB23H3 ARE REQUIRED to take
MGEB11H3 as EXTRA before enrolling themselves into MGEB12H3
Which course will be open to Non-Program Students and When
Non-Program students (including Economics Minor students) may enroll in MGEA02H3,
MGEA06H3 and MGEC93H3 from the start of course enrolment.

MGED90H3 (20255) — Supervised Reading
Enrollment
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been
granted. Check your status through ACORN to see whether you have been approved. (APP =
approval; REF = refused; INT = no decision yet)
Notes
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled
until you complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with the MGE faculty member who you hope will supervise your study/project and

obtain their approval. Make sure the course code, supervisor name, and title of the project is
input on the supervised study form as this information will appear on your transcript. The
Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form
Step 3: Once complete, send the approval email from the faculty member and the completed
Supervised Study form by email to the Academic Director, Economics ecoss.utsc@utoronto.ca
and Jacqueline Deane jacqueline.deane@utoronto.ca
Step 4: If your proposal is approved, the department will update the Registrar's Office with your
Supervised Study form. Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to
approved (APP).
Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork. See policy for more details: h
ttps://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/mgmt/sites/utsc.utoronto.ca.mgmt/files/docs/Departmental%20Pol
icy%20on%20Supervised%20Reading%20Courses%20(October%202023).pdf
Economics and Management Office IC250
Component Section Day Time Delivery Instructor
LEC 1 INPER

pursuing degree or program requirements. Please see Calendar for overall course load limit for
BBA students.

MGTD80H3 (20255) — Supervised Reading in Management
Enrollment
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been
granted. Check your status through ACORN to see whether you have been approved. (APP =
approval; REF = refused; INT = no decision yet)
Notes
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled
until you complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2: Meet with the MGT faculty member who you hope will supervise your study/project and
obtain their approval. Make sure the course code, supervisor name, and title of the project is
input on the supervised study form as this information will appear on your transcript. The
Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form
Step 3: Once complete, send the approval email from the faculty member and the completed
Supervised Study form by email to the Academic Director, Management
mgmtss.utsc@utoronto.ca and Jacqueline Deane jacqueline.deane@utoronto.ca
Step 4: If your proposal is approved, the department will update the Registrar's Office with your
Supervised Study form. Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to
approved (APP).
Your Department listed below may require additional paperwork. See policy for more details: h
ttps://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/mgmt/sites/utsc.utoronto.ca.mgmt/files/docs/Departmental%20Pol
icy%20on%20Supervised%20Reading%20Courses%20(October%202023).pdf
Economics and Management Office IC250
Component Section Day Time Delivery Instructor
LEC 1 INPER

Enrollment
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been
granted. Check your status through ACORN to see whether you have been approved. (APP =
approval; REF = refused; INT = no decision yet)
Notes
SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1:
Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled until
you complete the remaining steps (below).
Step 2:
Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure
the course code, supervisor name and title of the project is clearly printed on the form as this
information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Your Department listed below
may require additional paperwork. Students should contact the Office listed for more
information.

Step 3:
Please submit the signed Supervised Study form by email to Jason Ferreira
jason.ferreira@utoronto.ca.
Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).

Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'. Make sure
the course code, supervisor name and title of the project is clearly printed on the form as this
information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Your Department listed below
may require additional paperwork. Students should contact the Office listed for more
information.
Step 3:
Please submit the signed Supervised Study form by email to Jason Ferreira
jason.ferreira@utoronto.ca.
Staff will update your course status on ACORN from interim (INT) to approved (APP).

PHYD01H3 (20255) — Research Project in Physics and Astrophysics
Enrollment
Enrolment Indicator: A
Students request the course on ACORN but will not be officially enrolled until approval has been
granted. Check your status through ACORN to see whether you have been approved. (APP =
approval; REF = refused; INT = no decision yet)
Notes
SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
In order to qualify for a Supervised Study course, students must locate a professor who will
agree to supervise the course, and then follow the steps outlined below.
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled
until you complete the remaining steps.
Step 2: Fill the 'Student' section on a 'Supervised Study Form' available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form.
Step 3: Once you fill-in the 'Student' section, contact your Supervisor and provide them with
the form. Your supervisor will complete their section and forward the form for departmental
approval.
Step 4: Once the project is approved at the departmental level, the form will be submitted to
the Registrar's Office and your status on ACORN will be updated from interim (INT) to approved

(APP).
Component Section Day Time Delivery Instructor
LEC 1 INPER Valencia, D.

Health Studies + Neuroscience may only complete only 1.0 PSY/NRO D-level credits. Students
will be refused from PSY/NRO D-level enrollment beyond this limit. PSYD98 and NROD98 are
excluded from this requirement. Please see the following website for more information:

Notes
SUPERVISED STUDY/RESEARCH & INDEPENDENT STUDY COURSES
Step 1: Request the course on ACORN. Your status will be INT. You will not be officially enrolled
until you complete the remaining steps (below).

Step 2: Meet with the Supervisor and obtain their signature on a 'Supervised Study form'.
Ensure the course code, supervisor's name and title of the project is clearly printed on the form
as this information will appear on your transcript. The Supervised Study form is available at:
https://www.utsc.utoronto.ca/registrar/supervised-study-form. Your Department listed below
may require additional paperwork. Students should contact the office listed for more
information.
Step 3: Submit the signed Supervised Study form and additional paperwork by email to the
Program Advisor sociologyadvisor.utsc@utoronto.ca.
Your course status on ACORN will be updated from interim (INT) to approved (APP).
Sociology Advisor Office HL450
Component Section Day Time Delivery Instructor
LEC 1 INPER
